6  MODULE mode_read_xker_raccs
7 ! ###########################
8 IMPLICIT NONE
9 CONTAINS
10  SUBROUTINE read_xker_raccs (KACCLBDAS,KACCLBDAR,KND, &
11  PALPHAS,PNUS,PALPHAR,PNUR,PESR,PBS,PBR,PCS,PDS,PFVELOS,PCR,PDR, &

14 !DEC$ OPTIMIZE:0
15  USE yomhook , ONLY : lhook, dr_hook, jphook
16 ! ##########################################################################
17 !
18 !!**** * * - initialize the kernels for the rain-snow accretion process
19 !!
20 !! PURPOSE
21 !! -------
22 !! The purpose of this routine is to initialize the kernels PKER_RACCSS,
23 !! PKER_RACCS and PKER_SACCRG prepared from a previous run of the routine
24 !! INI_RAIN_ICE. The reading of the kernels is optional after checking for
25 !! the dimensions of the arrays.
26 !!
27 !!** METHOD
28 !! ------
29 !!
30 !!
31 !! EXTERNAL
32 !! --------
33 !! None
34 !!
35 !!
36 !! IMPLICIT ARGUMENTS
37 !! ------------------
38 !! None
39 !!
40 !! REFERENCE
41 !! ---------
42 !! Book2 of documentation ( routine READ_XKER_RACCS )
43 !!
44 !! AUTHOR
45 !! ------
46 !! J.-P. Pinty * Laboratoire d'Aerologie*
47 !!
48 !! MODIFICATIONS
49 !! -------------
50 !! Original 09/04/96
51 !! 14-Feb-2014 R. El Khatib optimise for compile time on Intel
52 !!
53 !-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
54 !
55 !* 0. DECLARATIONS
56 ! ------------
57 !
58 !* 0.2 Declarations of local variables :
59 !
60 !
61 INTEGER, INTENT(OUT) :: KND,KACCLBDAS,KACCLBDAR
62 REAL, INTENT(OUT) :: PALPHAS
63 REAL, INTENT(OUT) :: PNUS
64 REAL, INTENT(OUT) :: PALPHAR
65 REAL, INTENT(OUT) :: PNUR
66 REAL, INTENT(OUT) :: PESR
